Multipath TCP (MPTCP)

Draft agenda

Date: Monday, November 2, 2015, 9:00 - 11:30 (Morning Session I)
Room: 413

 - Intro - Chairs [15mins]
     Status Updates

 - MPTCP for FreeBSD update  - Grenville Armitage (5 mins)

 - Mptcp enduser use cases and enhancement opportunities - Chetan Harsha   (20 mins)
    (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-palanivelanchetan-mptcp-challenges-usecases"&gt;draft-palanivelanchetan-mptcp-challenges-usecases&lt;/a&gt;)

 - Making Multipath TCP robust for stateless webservers - Christoph Paasch (20 mins)
    (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-paasch-mptcp-syncookies"&gt;draft-paasch-mptcp-syncookies&lt;/a&gt;)

 - Multipath TCP behind Layer-4 loadbalancers - Christoph Paasch (15 mins)
    (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-paasch-mptcp-loadbalancer"&gt;draft-paasch-mptcp-loadbalancer&lt;/a&gt;)

 - Securing the MultiPath TCP handshake - Christoph Paasch (5 mins)

 - LISA: A Linked Slow-Start Algorithm for MPTCP  - Runa Barik              (20 mins)
    (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-barik-mptcp-lisa"&gt;draft-barik-mptcp-lisa&lt;/a&gt;)

DTN Working Group
IETF 94
Yokohama, Japan
November 3rd 2015

Primary objective: move forward rfc5050bis.
Note: we may not have time to cover all presentations. highest priority is rfc5050bis

Agenda:

1) Administrativia, co-chairs

2) RFC5050bis (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-dtnwg-bp"&gt;draft-dtnwg-bp&lt;/a&gt;), Scott Burleigh

3) SBSP (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-birrane-dtn-sbsp"&gt;draft-birrane-dtn-sbsp&lt;/a&gt;), Ed Birrane

4) Security Key Management (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-templin-dtnskmreq"&gt;draft-templin-dtnskmreq&lt;/a&gt;,&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-viswanathan-dtnwg-pkdn"&gt;draft-viswanathan-dtnwg-pkdn&lt;/a&gt;), Fred Templin

5) Network Management (&lt;a href="http://tools.ietf.org/html?draft=draft-birrane-dtn-amp"&gt;draft-birrane-dtn-amp&lt;/a&gt;*), Ed Birrane

6) Next steps (co-chairs)

    function set_location() {
	var now = new Date;
	var utc = now;
	utc.setMinutes(now.getMinutes() + now.getTimezoneOffset());
	var loc = utc;
	// Switch page location 1 hour after local time, to give stragglers some leeway.
	loc.setHours(utc.getHours() + 0 - 1);
	var localtime = loc.format("%Y-%m-%d_%H%M");
	var anchors = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
	for (var i = 0; i&lt;anchors.length;i++){
	    var anchor = anchors[i];
	    if (anchor.name &amp;&amp; anchor.name[0] == "2") {
		if ((anchor.name &gt; localtime)) {
		    window.location.hash = anchor.name;
		    break;
		}
	    }
	}
    }

    &lt;h3&gt;Monday November 2, 9:00&lt;/h3&gt;
    &lt;div class="indented"&gt;

&lt;dt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Agenda Bash &lt;/b&gt;&lt;/dt&gt;

      group (draft-&amp;lt;author&amp;gt;-v6ops-*), may be determined from &lt;a

&lt;pre&gt;



# HTTP Working Group Agenda - IETF 94

* [Meeting chat](xmpp:httpbis@jabber.ietf.org?join)
* [Minutes](&lt;a href="http://etherpad.tools.ietf.org:9000/p/ietf94-httpbis"&gt;http://etherpad.tools.ietf.org:9000/p/ietf94-httpbis&lt;/a&gt;)

*Taking minutes? See [our guide](&lt;a href="https://github.com/httpwg/wiki/wiki/TakingMinutes"&gt;https://github.com/httpwg/wiki/wiki/TakingMinutes&lt;/a&gt;)*


## Monday, 2 November 2015 13:00-15:00

### Administrivia

* 2 min - Blue sheets / scribe selection / NOTE WELL
* 3 min - Agenda bashing


### Specification Status

*5 minutes*

Discuss current status of approved and recently published specifications.


### [Alternative Services](&lt;a href="https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-alt-svc"&gt;https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-alt-svc&lt;/a&gt;)

*20 minutes*

Discuss the [issues list](&lt;a href="https://github"&gt;https://github&lt;/a&gt;.com/httpwg/http-extensions/issues?q=is%3Aopen+is%3Aissue+label%3Aalt-svc) and draft status.


### [Opportunistic Security](&lt;a href="https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-http2-encryption"&gt;https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-ietf-httpbis-http2-encryption&lt;/a&gt;)

*10 minutes*

Discuss the [issues list](&lt;a href="https://github"&gt;https://github&lt;/a&gt;.com/httpwg/http-extensions/issues?q=is%3Aopen+is%3Aissue+label%3Aopp-sec) and draft status.


### Client Certificates and HTTP/2

*30 minutes*

Discuss [proposals for Client Certificate support in HTTP/2](&lt;a href="https://github.com/httpwg/wiki/wiki/H2ClientCerts"&gt;https://github.com/httpwg/wiki/wiki/H2ClientCerts&lt;/a&gt;).


### Potential Work

*balance of time*

Discuss possible [future work items](&lt;a href="https://github.com/httpwg/wiki/wiki/WatchList"&gt;https://github.com/httpwg/wiki/wiki/WatchList&lt;/a&gt;)


### wrap-up

* 5 minutes

&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/body&gt;&lt;/html&gt;

&lt;!--/*--&gt;&lt;![CDATA[/*&gt;&lt;!--*/
 function CodeHighlightOn(elem, id)
 {
   var target = document.getElementById(id);
   if(null != target) {
     elem.cacheClassElem = elem.className;
     elem.cacheClassTarget = target.className;
     target.className = "code-highlighted";
     elem.className   = "code-highlighted";
   }
 }
 function CodeHighlightOff(elem, id)
 {
   var target = document.getElementById(id);
   if(elem.cacheClassElem)
     elem.className = elem.cacheClassElem;
   if(elem.cacheClassTarget)
     target.className = elem.cacheClassTarget;
 }
/*]]&gt;*///--&gt;
&lt;/script&gt;
&lt;/head&gt;
